I was born and raised in Concord and my family has been coming here for over 30 years! These are truly the best donuts in the Bay Area. The owners are very kind and good to their customers. I lost my wallet a while back and the day after I called since it was the last place i‚Äôd been and YES they said they had seen it on the ground, I was the last customer they had before closing. <pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP3-PQlo0VHt1vFatqzQrEARnL4qe7-x1dxZxNV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMDEJRmpW-nVr7BHqbs7kuYXr_WaRKH_UMz0g3g=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPAjdG15XLez2qH54m1KHK60WkRS7WmPreCWAl9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures>< GmapID>
0x808f86cdab581373:0x3950cf55327bc0bf<//GmapID>
< Review>
Little Joe's is the sleeper neighborhood restaurant. A very unassuming sliver of what appears to be your run-of-the-mill greasy Chinese spoon establishment actually turns out some fantastic Cantonese cuisine.

With a 5 year old, our standard test Chinese fare (to see where this particular restaurant falls on our scale) is fairly, well, standard,  but they are executed well here.

The house special fried rice comes with diced bbq pork, sections of chicken thigh meat, slices of beef, and 3 or 4 large prawns. The dish isn't too greasy, didn't taste of stale cooking oil, and doesn't leave a pool of oil on the plate, which means the chef is cooking with high heat and a swift hand.

Cashew nut chicken and broccoli beef are our other yardstick dishes, and Little Joe's are served with satisfyingly fresh ingredients. The cashew chicken had evenly cooked vibrant zucchini, celery, and a few button mushroom halves. No old, yellowed celery stems or squishy squash past it's prime, and a very generous scattering of cashews that didn't force us to ration each scoop.

The beef with broccoli had tons of fresh, crisp broccoli (almost too crisp, could have used 30 seconds more cooking time!) And thankfully, slices of tender beef that hadn't been given the usual Cantonese treatment of  baking soda to puff it up. I'm not a fan of pillowy puffy beef so they win points for leaving the beef and chicken unadulterated!

The establishment is small and very bare-bones; we ate under a flourescent light with a tv showing a sportsball game so the gem√ºtlichkeit, or ambiance was not supreme, but the food was done very well and we knew what to expect.  Take-out seems to be the preferred way of enjoying their food, but don't be dissuaded by their sparse dining room!<//Review>

<review>Great place to buy a Subaru - especially if you're shopping around used. I walked out with a 2013 Subaru STI at a great price. They replaced all the major parts at 95k miles such as the timing belt.

Marcus was especially helpful and provided both CarFax  AND an AutoCheck full report. Car was well maintained throughout the life span and was serviced every few months. Marcus recommended that I brought my own mechanic and so I did. The STI being a used car wasn't perfect cosmetically (which is OK for an 8 year old car!) but everything seemed to check out - my mechanic used an advanced OB2 scanner and found out that they weren't hiding any code sensors. Brake pads weren't amazing, but rotors were still in good shape and Marcus offered his mechanics to get that replaced.

Fred seems like a very knowledgeable mechanic when it comes to working on Subarus as well, and they were all very welcoming and transparent throughout the transaction.

I'm typically very hesitant and on my guard about buying a used performance car, however these guys seem to really specialize in the niche of performance vehicles - and I'd highly recommend checking them out if that is what you're in the market for.

Also wanted to note that they are only looking to work with serious buyers - if you're window shopping and just want to test drive a car for fun, this place might not be for you. They offer financing but for older vehicles, you may want to look at Credit Union pre approvals from places like Mission Federal and Navy Federal CU.

I've been incredibly happy with my car and this is the most powerful ride I've driven. Thank you SD Auto Club for making performance affordable!</review><Pictures>None<//Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><Gmap_id>0x80d950c7a16bf6ed:0xf4fc64284548ad0b<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<user_id>103684718096621823802< /user_id><Name>Dana A Cruz</Name><date>1464985682993</date><Rating>1< /Rating>< text>
Let's just start by talking about bate and switch. My husband found a black 2006 Subaru STI online at San Diego Auto Club . It looked great online, pretty much sold it self by looks and mileage. We knew we still needed to check the engine and test drive. So we stop in and talk to a guy named Marcus, Husband test drives it and notices the touch screen radio was replaced with a single DIN radio. When we asked,  we were told "oh yeah, that thing it didn't even work, it wouldn't turn on." Then said, "but if you want it we can put it back on for you". We found torn audiowires in the back seat. The fuse box cover was missing and the front passenger door didn't open from the outside. In the original picture the spoiler had perrin fins. But those to were missing. And the HKS exhaust was replace with an ebay exhaust. Now on to the engine...the ingine intake was missing and was replaced with a Cobb intake. Bolts missing from the intercooler. Intercooler was loose as well as coolant catch can. Radiator was a automatic unit instead of a manual.  Coolant residue on engine, indicating a Coolant leak. And some clamps missing from hoses. The spare tire and Jack were also missing. Front  bumper was loose. Inner edge wear on the tires. Car was to be sold for 17995. High for blue book ....Bottom line thank God my Husbands a mechanic and knows what to look for. If buying a car with them, I recommend you take a mechanic with you or take it to a dealership for a pre purchase inspection.<//text>

Dr. Kevin Barry was recommended to me by a friend who has been his patient for over 20 years. On my first visit he spotted what turned out to be a root canal emergency (completely overlooked by previous dentist). He set up an appointment with a root canal specialist 2 blocks away who did the surgery that afternoon. Dr. K. Barry has the latest technology and the expertise/experience to match. He's the best dentist I've ever had, and I'm pretty old (60+). He's a lover of small talk, which puts me at ease during procedures. Always has a smile on his face and is willing to help. I've never seen him have a negative interaction with anyone. His staff will bend over backwards to set you up with a convenient appointment. They are excellent communicators (text, email, etc.)  Covid guidelines are in place. Dr. Barry also knows a network of highly competent dentists of various specialties to recommend for additional work you may need, which is a Plus in any profession! The best...A++ 8 years and still impressed!</review>

First of all, they're in the beautiful, Pflueger-designed, easy-to-get-to 450 Sutter building, which makes going in a pleasure in itself. Pat Huey</Name>
<Date>1568130645207</Date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
<Review>I have bruxism (tooth grinding) and Dr Daniel Barry gave me the perfect solution: sleep on your back. That way your neck and jaw relax and it eliminates the problem of grinding. He said when you sleep on your side, your neck is at an angle and this adds stress to it, which can trigger the bruxism. He also suggested a yogic breathing exercise (pranayama), and a couple of other non-druggie suggestions. (If you do yoga, a supported shoulder stand, which Mr Iyengar called the mother of all asanas, is excellent for anxiety and sleep problems.) What other dentist would come up with these kinds of suggestions? I wish I had known about them years ago. I've been doing them and sleep much better, and I am pretty sure that I'm no longer grinding at night.

He did an implant and two crowns for me (both resulting from the horrid bruxism) and did a perfect job. One of the crowns was put in by another dentist who had not done a great job (in fact, I'm pretty sure it was unnecessary, and it only lasted two years) and he did a great job working around the problems the bad dentist had caused. The mouth guard I bought fits perfectly.

The staff are always pleasant, cheerful, and competent.

My friend who recommended the Barrys has been going to them for 27 years. I wish I had known about them 27 years ago!</Review>< Pics>

After visiting several storage facilities, including another Extra Space Storage location, I actually chose this facility because, Katherine, the manager at this location was extremely friendly and helpful when I first stopped by to inquire about rates for a storage unit. The other locations lacked any kind of personal connection and friendly service. I felt like I was just another number filling another numbered space.
